Keywords: 
cesar anniversary workers 

Final sequence:

Mr. Chairman, I rise in support of the bill H.R. 2589, the ``Copyright Term Extension Act of 1995.'' I wish to commend the bill's sponsors for their work on this issue and urge them to continue to work on the Copyright Term Extension Act.  The purpose of the Copyright Term Extension Act is simple: to extend the statutory term of the ``fair use'' exception, established in the first Congress of this Republic, so that every new song or phrase that enters our culture during the next 10 years will continue to have the statutory rights of the author and the publisher.  Unfortunately, the Copyright Term Extension Act has been too frequently interpreted to include too much new copyright terms. The Copyright Term Extension Act is intended to be temporary. A motion to reconsider was laid on the table.<|endoftext|><|endoftext|><|endoftext|><|endoftext|><|endoftext|><|endoftext|><|endoftext|><|endoftext|><|endoftext|><|endoftext|><|endoftext|><|endoftext|><|endoftext|><|endoftext|><|endoftext|><|endoftext|><|endoftext|><|endoftext|><|endoftext|><|endoftext|><|endoftext|><|endoftext|><|endoftext|><|endoftext|><|endoftext|><|endoftext|><|endoftext|><|endoftext|>
